Given an empty chat log, starting a conversation is a natural first step. The agent must choose exactly one action per turn from MOVE, SAY, or WAIT.

- **MOVE** would change the agent's position but would not directly initiate social interaction. While moving closer to some players could be useful later, it isn't necessary for a greeting because the nearby players are already within range. Additionally, moving without greeting might miss the chance to connect immediately.
- **WAIT** does nothing and fails to advance the goal of being social.
- **SAY** directly fulfills the greeting objective. A single greeting can address all nearby players at once, which is efficient and friendly.

Thus, the best course is to use **SAY** with a warm, inclusive message like "Hello everyone!" to greet all players in the vicinity. This action aligns with the goal of being interesting and starts building social presence right away.
